CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS move(
   MOVE_ID      INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,TYPE_ID      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,CATEGORY_ID  INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,MOVE_NAME    VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL
  ,MOVER_PWR    INTEGER 
  ,MOVE_ACC     INTEGER 
  ,MOVE_PP      INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,MOVE_EFFECT  VARCHAR(240)
  ,MOVE_EF_PROB INTEGER
  ,FOREIGN KEY (TYPE_ID) REFERENCES typings(TYPE_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (CATEGORY_ID) REFERENCES category(CATEGORY_ID)
);

   SPECIES_NUM  INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,SPECIES_NAME VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS p_egg(
   SPECIES_NUM INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,GROUP_ID    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,PRIMARY KEY(SPECIES_NUM,GROUP_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (SPECIES_NUM) REFERENCES p_species(SPECIES_NUM)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (GROUP_ID) REFERENCES egg_group(GROUP_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS form(
   SPECIES_NUM     INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_ID         INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,REGION_ID       INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_NAME       VARCHAR(36)
  ,FORM_BASE_HP    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_BASE_ATK   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_BASE_DEF   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_BASE_SPATK INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_BASE_SPDEF INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_BASE_SPD   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,PRIMARY KEY(SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (SPECIES_NUM) REFERENCES p_species(SPECIES_NUM)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (REGION_ID) REFERENCES region(REGION_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS p_type(
   SPECIES_NUM INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_ID     INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,TYPE_ID     INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,PRIMARY KEY(SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID,TYPE_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID) REFERENCES form(SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (TYPE_ID) REFERENCES typings(TYPE_ID)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS pokemon(
   POKE_ID       INTEGER  NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY 
  ,TRAINER_ID    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,SPECIES_NUM   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,FORM_ID       INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,NATURE_ID     INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,POKEMON_SHINY BIT  NOT NULL
  ,FOREIGN KEY (TRAINER_ID) REFERENCES trainer(TRAINER_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID) REFERENCES form(SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID)
  ,FOREIGN KEY (NATURE_ID) REFERENCES nature(NATURE_ID)
);

INSERT INTO pokemon(TRAINER_ID,SPECIES_NUM,FORM_ID,NATURE_ID,POKEMON_SHINY) VALUES (12664,442,0,16,0);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS iv(
   POKE_ID  INTEGER  NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY 
  ,IV_HP    INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,IV_ATK   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,IV_DEF   INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,IV_SPATK INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,IV_SPDEF INTEGER  NOT NULL
  ,IV_SPD   INTEGER  NOT NULL
);

);
